If the trump is chosen in the first round you receive the trump card and must shed any card you wish.\r\n‚úì\tThe player next to the dealer in a clock-wise direction is the first to choose a trump suit. \r\n‚úì\tIf that player passes the chance, the next one after him follows.\r\n‚úì\tThe game is played between two teams: a top-bottom team comprised of you and a computer player and a left-right team of computer players.\r\n‚úì\tThe player and his partner are called the makers if one of them chooses a trump suit. Otherwise they are called the defenders.\r\n‚úì\tTo win the makers must take at least 3 tricks. The defenders in order to win must take at least 3 tricks as well.\r\n‚úì\tIf the makers take 5 tricks they score 2 points. If the defenders take 3 or more tricks they score 2 points.\r\n‚úì\tIf the makers take 3 or 4 tricks they score 1 point. If the makers take less than 3 tricks they score 0 points.\r\n‚úì\tThere is the possibility of playing alone by pressing the -play alone- button when choosing the trump.\r\n‚úì\tWhen playing alone the team scores 4 points if the maker takes all 5 tricks.
